 pakistan ke liye das bindu vaale target is prakaar hai-1
 Demonstrate that the risks of terrorism funding have been properly identified, assessed and monitored based on risk-sensitivity
 2
 Show that remedial actions and sanctions have been applied in cases of violation of the Anti Money Laundering and Countering Financing of Terrorism Act 2009 (AML / CFT Act) and that these actions have an impact on the compliance of AML / CFT by financial institutions 
 3
 Demonstrate that competent authorities are cooperating and taking action to identify and enforce illegal money or value transfer service
 4
 Ensure that the illegal movement of currency and identification of cash couriers is ensured
 5
 Ensure inter-agency coordination between the provincial and federal authorities in the matter of dealing with terrorist financing
 6
 Ensure that law enforcement agencies are catching up with the activities of Terror Financing
 7
 Ensure that Terror Financing can be stopped by Terror Financing lawsuits
 8
 Identify and seize assets that promote Terror funding
 9
 Ensure that those who violate these provisions are punished by criminal cases
 10
 Deny the funding bases or institutions of funding from their resources

 - pravara, purana, manjara, benganga aadi isaki sahaayak nadiyaan hai
 26
 kaverikarnataka ke kurg jile main sthit brahm giri paharibengal kii khadiiski kul lambaai 800 kilometre he-samudra tal se isaki unchai 1341 meter he- ise dakshin bharat kii ganga ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 - The presence of Sivasamudram Jalapratap Srirangapatam hinders its importance
